Abstract: While recent reductions of zero-sum partially observable stochastic games (zs-POSGs) to transition-independent stochastic games (TI-SGs) theoretically admit dynamic programming, practical solutions remain stifled by the inherent non-linearity and exponential complexity of the simultaneous minimax backup. In this work, we surmount this computational barrier by rigorously recasting the simultaneous interaction as a sequential decision process via the principle of separation. We introduce distinct sufficient statistics for valuation and execution, the sequential occupancy state and the private occupancy family, which reveal a latent geometry in the optimal value function. This structural insight allows us to linearise the backup operator, reducing the update complexity from exponential to polynomial while enabling the direct extraction of safe policies without heuristic bookkeeping. Experimental results demonstrate that algorithms leveraging this sequential framework significantly outperform state-of-the-art methods, effectively rendering previously intractable domains solvable.

### [123] [Fair Division Under Inaccurate Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24169)
*Trung Dang,Daniel Halpern,Anuran Makur,Alexandros Psomas,Japneet Singh,Paritosh Verma*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在个体偏好存在不准确性的情况下，不可分割物品的公平分配问题，重点关注最小化嫉妒。考虑了真实偏好和噪声的随机性与最坏情况组合，提出了不同设置下的算法保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公平分配稀缺资源是数学、计算机科学、运筹学和经济学中的核心问题。现有公平分配文献大多假设个体具有基数偏好，但获取精确数值偏好通常认知负担重且容易出错。虽然已有研究关注序数偏好，但其表达能力有限，难以量化和优化嫉妒等基数公平目标。

Method: 论文探索了在基数偏好不准确情况下不可分割物品公平分配的广泛场景。考虑了四种设置组合：真实偏好（随机/最坏情况）×噪声（随机/最坏情况）。针对不同设置：1）随机真实偏好下，证明高概率计算无嫉妒分配；2）最坏情况偏好和有限噪声下，分析Round-Robin算法的最大嫉妒界限；3）最坏情况偏好和噪声下，提出在线算法，在分配时揭示物品真实偏好，保证对数级最大嫉妒。

Result: 1）随机真实偏好下（无论噪声随机或最坏情况），都能高概率计算无嫉妒分配，推广了无噪声随机公平分配的已有结果。2）最坏情况偏好和有限噪声下，给出了Round-Robin算法的最大嫉妒界限，证明对确定性算法是紧的。3）最坏情况偏好和噪声下，提出高效在线算法，高概率保证对数级最大嫉妒，将算法差异理论推广到噪声输入数据场景。

Conclusion: 论文系统研究了偏好不准确性对公平分配的影响，在不同偏好和噪声假设下提供了算法保证。结果表明，即使在偏好信息不完整或不准确的情况下，仍能实现良好的公平性保证，扩展了公平分配理论对现实世界不完美偏好信息的处理能力。

Abstract: The fair allocation of scarce resources is a central problem in mathematics, computer science, operations research, and economics. While much of the fair-division literature assumes that individuals have underlying cardinal preferences, eliciting exact numerical values is often cognitively burdensome and prone to inaccuracies. A growing body of work in fair division addresses this challenge by assuming access only to ordinal preferences. However, the restricted expressiveness of ordinal preferences makes it challenging to quantify and optimize cardinal fairness objectives such as envy.
  In this paper, we explore the broad landscape of fair division of indivisible items given inaccurate cardinal preferences, with a focus on minimizing envy. We consider various settings based on whether the true preferences of the agents are stochastic or worst-case, and whether the inaccuracies, modeled as additive noise, are stochastic or worst-case. When the true preferences are stochastic, we show that envy-free allocations can be computed with high probability; this is achieved both in the setting with stochastic and worst-case noise. This generalizes a notable result in stochastic fair division, which establishes a similar guarantee, albeit in the absence of any noise. When the true preferences are worst-case, and the noise is bounded, we analyze the maximum envy achieved by the Round-Robin algorithm. This bound is shown to be tight for deterministic algorithms, and applications of this bound are provided. Lastly, we consider a setting with worst-case preferences and noise, where the true preferences for each item are revealed upon its allocation. Here, we give an efficient online algorithm that guarantees logarithmic maximum envy with high probability. This result generalizes a known result from algorithmic discrepancy to a setting with noisy input data.

In particular, we are interested in those disturbances that are able to flip a decision made by the agent. Such a disturbance may, for instance, occur when the intended action of the agent cannot be executed due to a malfunction of an actuator in the environment. In this work, we introduce the concept of resilience in the stochastic setting and present a comprehensive set of fundamental problems. Specifically, we discuss such problems for Markov decision processes with reachability and safety objectives, which also smoothly extend to stochastic games. To account for the stochastic setting, we provide various ways of aggregating the amounts of disturbances that may have occurred, for instance, in expectation or in the worst case. Moreover, to reason about infinite disturbances, we use quantitative measures, like their frequency of occurrence.

Our main information-theoretic results are compact and self-contained: an exact capacity theorem ($C_0=1$), a tight side-information lower bound for resolution ($\geq\log_2 k$ bits for $k$-way incoherence), and a rate--complexity separation (modification cost $O(1)$ at capacity vs $Ω(n)$ above).
  The paper frames encoding locations as terminals in a multi-terminal source-coding model. Derivation (automatic deterministic dependence) is interpreted as perfect correlation that reduces effective rate; only complete derivation (one independent source) achieves zero incoherence. We give concise achievability and converse proofs in IT style, formalize the confusability/incoherence graph connection, and present an explicit mutual-information argument for the side-information bound.
  Theoretical contributions are supplemented by constructive instantiations (programming-language patterns and a software case study). For TIT submission we move detailed language evaluation, extended code examples, and the full Lean proof corpus to supplementary material; the main text contains brief instantiations only. ### [126] [On the Uniqueness of Solutions in GPS Source Localization: Distance and Squared-Distance Minimization under Limited Measurements in Two and Three Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23741)

Furthermore, we discuss the number of possible source solutions when the number of measurements is fewer than three.

</details>


### [127] [Are Stacked Intelligent Metasurfaces (SIMs) Better than Single-layer Reconfigurable Intelligent Surfaces (RISs) for Wideband Multi-user MIMO Communication Systems?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23534)
*Muhammad Ibrahim,Amine Mezghani,Ekram Hossain*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一个考虑耦合效应的宽带电路模型，用于分析级联智能超表面(SIMs)，并设计了联合主动和被动波束成形方案以最大化频谱效率。研究表明，在宽带多用户场景下，SIMs能显著优于单层RIS，而部分可重构SIM架构能以较低复杂度实现接近最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层可重构智能表面(RISs)在宽带无线通信中存在物理限制，级联智能超表面(SIMs)通过智能操控电磁波来增强复杂环境中的信号传播，并提供额外的波束成形自由度。需要建立考虑频率相关互耦合和宽带信道响应的模型来优化系统性能。

Method: 提出了一个耦合感知的宽带电路框架，捕捉多个子带上的频率相关互耦合和宽带信道响应。基于此模型，制定了联合主动和被动波束成形设计，优化基站预编码器以实现跨频率选择性子带的载波聚合，同时优化超表面相移以最大化频谱效率。

Result: 仿真结果表明，考虑耦合和宽带效应至关重要，性能强烈依赖于操作条件。在窄带和/或低信噪比条件下，单层RIS配置可能更有利；而在宽带多用户条件下，SIMs通过减轻耦合引起的失真并保持更一致的跨频率相位响应，能显著优于单层RIS。部分可重构SIM架构能以降低的复杂度实现接近最优性能。

Conclusion: SIMs是未来宽带多用户MIMO系统的可扩展解决方案，在结构简单性和宽带适应性之间存在设计权衡。部分可重构SIM架构在性能和复杂度之间提供了良好平衡，为实际部署提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: Cascaded or stacked intelligent metasurfaces (SIMs) have emerged as a promising technology to overcome the physical limitations of single-layer reconfigurable intelligent surfaces (RISs) in wideband wireless communication. By intelligently manipulating electromagnetic waves, SIMs enhance signal propagation in complex environments and offer additional degrees of freedom for beamforming. This paper proposes a coupling-aware, wideband, circuit-based framework that captures frequency-dependent mutual coupling and wideband channel responses over multiple subbands. Based on this model, we formulate a joint active and passive beamforming design that optimizes the base-station precoder to enable carrier aggregation across frequency-selective subbands, together with metasurface phase shifts, to maximize spectral efficiency. Simulation results reveal the importance of accounting for coupling and wideband effects, and show that performance depends strongly on operating conditions. Single-layer RIS configurations can be favorable in narrowband and/or low-SNR regimes, whereas SIMs can significantly outperform under wideband multi-user conditions by mitigating coupling-induced distortion and maintaining a more consistent phase response across frequencies. The results provide physical insights into design trade-offs between structural simplicity and wideband adaptability, highlighting SIMs as a scalable solution for future-generation wideband multi-user MIMO systems. We further show that partially reconfigurable SIM architectures achieve near-optimal performance with reduced complexity.

</details>


### [128] [The Distance Spectrum of IEEE 802.11 Binary Convolutional Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23651)
*Rethna Pulikkoonattu*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文分析了IEEE 802.11标准中使用的二进制卷积编码（BCC）的距离谱计算，包括母码（码率1/2，K=7）及其三种标准穿孔衍生码（码率2/3、3/4、5/6），并推导了AWGN信道下的误比特率和误帧率性能界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LDPC码在高吞吐量应用中占主导地位，但BCC在IEEE 802.11标准中仍然至关重要，特别是在向后兼容性、带宽受限和成本敏感的应用中。BCC在Wi-Fi 6和即将到来的Wi-Fi 8标准中继续发挥重要作用，特别是在ELR数据包格式中。理解BCC在Viterbi解码下的性能需要准确计算其距离谱。

Method: 论文提出了精确计算IEEE 802.11 BCC母码（码率1/2，K=7，生成器八进制133/171）及其三种标准穿孔衍生码距离谱的方法。使用并集界推导了AWGN信道下BPSK/QPSK和Gray编码M-QAM调制的误比特率和误帧率曲线，并通过蒙特卡洛仿真进行验证。

Result: 提供了完整的距离谱计算结果，包括并集界性能曲线。这些结果通过蒙特卡洛仿真验证，表明理论分析与实际性能一致。论文还提供了Python、Julia和C++的开源实现。

Conclusion: BCC在IEEE 802.11标准中仍然具有持续的重要性，特别是在向后兼容性和资源受限的应用中。精确的距离谱计算为评估BCC性能提供了理论基础，开源实现促进了相关研究和应用开发。

Abstract: Binary convolutional coding (BCC) has been a cornerstone of the IEEE 802.11 wireless LAN standard since its inception, and it remains relevant today across the full generational arc from the legacy 802.11a/g through Wi-Fi 6 (802.11ax) and into the forthcoming Wi-Fi 8 (802.11bn). Although low-density parity-check (LDPC) codes now dominate high-throughput applications, BCC is mandatory for backward compatibility and continues to serve as the default forward-error-correction scheme in bandwidth-constrained and cost-sensitive deployments: 20 MHz-only devices, Internet-of-Things nodes, and other implementations where LDPC's decoder complexity is prohibitive. Critically, BCC at rate 1/2 is the coding scheme used throughout the packet preamble in every IEEE 802.11-compliant frame, making it indispensable regardless of which data-field code is selected. Furthermore, the new Enhanced Long Range (ELR) packet format introduced in the 802.11bn/UHR amendment mandates rate-1/2 BCC for the data portion of the frame, reinforcing the continued importance of this code in next-generation deployments. The performance of BCC under Viterbi decoding is governed by the distance spectrum of the convolutional code. This note explains how to compute that spectrum exactly for the IEEE 802.11 mother code (rate 1/2, K=7, generators octal 133 / octal 171) and its three standard punctured derivatives (rates 2/3, 3/4, 5/6) obtained via rate-compatible puncturing. Union-bound BEP and FER curves are derived for AWGN with BPSK/QPSK and Gray-coded M-QAM modulation and validated against Monte Carlo simulation. Python, Julia, and C++ implementations are openly available at https://github.com/geekymode/bcc_spectrum.

</details>


### [129] [Weighted Unequal Error Protection over a Rayleigh Fading Channel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24225)
*Adeel Mahmood*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究信道编码中的不等错误保护变体，分析两种可实现方案（功率域叠加和正交资源分配）在准静态瑞利衰落信道下的渐近和有限码长性能，发现功率域叠加优于正交资源分配但差距小于2%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究信道编码中不等错误保护的一种变体，其中消息比特串被划分为有限数量的块，优化目标是各块解码成功概率的加权和。在准静态瑞利衰落信道下，接收端已知信道状态信息而发送端未知，需要分析不同方案的性能。

Method: 采用两种可实现方案：基于功率域叠加（PDS）的方案和基于正交资源分配（ORA，即时分复用）的方案。推导了最优传输块数的上界，给出了计算两种方案最优功率和时间分配的算法，以及计算局部最优分配的简化算法。

Result: PDS方案性能优于ORA方案，但两者性能差异在渐近和有限码长情况下均小于2%。对于PDS和ORA，数值结果显示渐近性能与有限码长性能之间的差距上界：n=1000时约为10%，n=5000时约为3%。

Conclusion: 在准静态瑞利衰落信道下，功率域叠加方案在不等错误保护方面优于正交资源分配方案，但性能优势有限（小于2%）。两种方案的渐近与有限码长性能差距随码长增加而减小，为实际系统设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We study a variant of unequal error protection in channel coding, where the message bit string is divided into a finite number of blocks and the maximization objective is a weighted sum of per-block decoding success probabilities. The channel model is quasi-static Rayleigh fading with channel state information available to the receiver but unavailable to the transmitter. We analyze the asymptotic and finite blocklength performance of two achievability schemes, one based on power-domain superposition (PDS) and another based on orthogonal resource allocation (ORA), also known as time-sharing. Upper bounds on the optimal number of blocks to transmit are derived. Algorithms to compute the optimal power and time splits for the two schemes are given. Simplified algorithms to compute locally optimal power and time splits are also given, and their outputs match those of the previous algorithms across all tested parameters. Our results show that PDS outperforms ORA, but the performance differential is less than 2% in both the asymptotic and finite blocklength regimes (Figures 4 - 6). For both PDS and ORA, numerical results also upper bound the gap between the asymptotic and finite blocklength performance by approximately 10% for n = 1000 and 3% for n = 5000 (Figures 7 - 10).

### [130] [Finite Block Length Rate-Distortion Theory for the Bernoulli Source with Hamming Distortion: A Tutorial](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24243)
*Bhaskar Krishnamachari*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 关于伯努利序列在汉明失真下的率失真理论的教程，涵盖经典RD函数推导、Blahut-Arimoto算法计算，以及有限块长下的率失真弥散分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 香农率失真理论虽然提供了数据压缩的基本极限，但假设无限长块长，这在实践中无法实现。需要研究有限块长下的实际压缩性能，特别是如何逼近香农极限。

Method: 针对最简单的非平凡信源——伯努利(p)序列，在汉明失真度量下：1) 从基本原理推导经典率失真函数RD = Hp - HD；2) 使用Blahut-Arimoto算法进行数值计算；3) 分析有限块长下的率失真弥散V(D)，研究最小可实现速率如何以O(1/√n)的惩罚逼近香农极限。

Result: 建立了伯努利序列在汉明失真下的完整率失真理论框架，包括经典RD函数、数值计算方法，以及有限块长下的弥散分析。通过Python脚本生成了数值示例和图表，验证了理论结果。

Conclusion: 该教程为理解率失真理论提供了自包含的入门，特别强调了有限块长下的实际压缩性能。率失真弥散V(D)是理解有限块长惩罚的关键量，支配着最小可实现速率以O(1/√n)的速度逼近香农极限。

Abstract: Lossy data compression lies at the heart of modern communication and storage systems. Shannon's rate-distortion theory provides the fundamental limit on how much a source can be compressed at a given fidelity, but it assumes infinitely long block lengths that are never realized in practice. We present a self-contained tutorial on rate-distortion theory for the simplest non-trivial source: a Bernoulli$(p)$ sequence with Hamming distortion. We derive the classical rate-distortion function $RD = Hp - HD$ from first principles, illustrate its computation via the Blahut-Arimoto algorithm, and then develop the finite block length refinements that characterize how the minimum achievable rate approaches the Shannon limit as the block length $n$ grows. The central quantity in this refinement is the \emph{rate-distortion dispersion} $V(D)$, which governs the $O(1/\sqrt{n})$ penalty for operating at finite block lengths. We accompany all theoretical developments with numerical examples and figures generated by accompanying Python scripts.

</details>
